Alex wasn't the name I was given at birth, but that's a different story. My mom had always told me that the reason my dad wasn't here was because he had gone MIA in Afghanistan. Throughout my entire life, I always knew I was different. I didn't fit in with the kids my mom wanted me to play with, and I was always getting dirty and getting into rough fights with bigger kids almost twice my size, and I somehow won every single fight I got into. Occasionally through the buildings I would see creatures (which I later learned were monsters) watching me through classroom windows or stalking me on the playground. As I grew older, I started to feel like I didn't belong even more. Like there was no place for me. I also started to realize that everything I had ever known about my dad seemed a little.... Off. I didn't even know his name, my mom refused to tell me, and we only had one picture in the house that was all burned at the edges. But because my mom is a difficult person, I didn't ask those questions. Finally, one day, I told my mom about me feeling like I didn't belong and feeling like I was born into the wrong body. She started screaming at me and throwing things, and practically disowned me, and that night I ran away. I didn't know what to do or where to go, or how I even made it to Long Island, but I eventually was chased by monsters all the way to camp. When I got to camp I introduced myself as the name I wanted to be called, which was Alex, and Ares claimed me a few days after I got there. I was still fighting to become who I truly was, as people were starting to suspect that I wasn't who I said I was, but then my dad came to visit me in a dream. Comment: datdudemr601 said "Raiders to cut ties with LaMarr Woodley after one year

Dan Hanzus
Around the NFL Writer
The LaMarr Woodley experiment in Oakland will begin and end with a whimper.

NFL Media Insider Ian Rapoport reported Sunday that the Raiders do not plan to pick up Woodley's $1 million roster bonus before the league deadline and will release the veteran linebacker, according to a source informed of the Raiders' thinking.

CSN Bay Area's Fallon Smith had the first report.

Woodley, 30, signed a two-year, $12 million contract with the Raiders last March in a move that typified a period of questionable spending by general manager Reggie McKenzie. Woodley played at a subpar level before being shelved for the final 10 games of the season with a biceps injury.

Woodley's game has been in regression for years, and he could struggle to find work on the open market. As for McKenzie, we'll soon find out if misfires like Woodley will change how he approaches free agency.

The latest Around The NFL Podcast breaks down the annual "Top 101 free agents" list and discusses the latest in league news. Find more Around The NFL content on NFL NOW."

NFL Media Insider Ian Rapoport reported Sunday that the Raiders do not plan to pick up Woodley's $1 million roster bonus before the league deadline and will release the veteran linebacker, according to a source informed of the Raiders' thinking.

CSN Bay Area's Fallon Smith had the first report.

Woodley, 30, signed a two-year, $12 million contract with the Raiders last March in a move that typified a period of questionable spending by general manager Reggie McKenzie. Woodley played at a subpar level before being shelved for the final 10 games of the season with a biceps injury.

Woodley's game has been in regression for years, and he could struggle to find work on the open market. As for McKenzie, we'll soon find out if misfires like Woodley will change how he approaches free agency.

The latest Around The NFL Podcast breaks down the annual "Top 101 free agents" list and discusses the latest in league news. Find more Around The NFL content on NFL NOW."

Comment: datdudemr601 said "Raiders to cut ties with LaMarr Woodley after one year

Dan Hanzus
Around the NFL Writer
The LaMarr Woodley experiment in Oakland will begin and end with a whimper.

NFL Media Insider Ian Rapoport reported Sunday that the Raiders do not plan to pick up Woodley's $1 million roster bonus before the league deadline and will release the veteran linebacker, according to a source informed of the Raiders' thinking.

CSN Bay Area's Fallon Smith had the first report.

Woodley, 30, signed a two-year, $12 million contract with the Raiders last March in a move that typified a period of questionable spending by general manager Reggie McKenzie. Woodley played at a subpar level before being shelved for the final 10 games of the season with a biceps injury.

Woodley's game has been in regression for years, and he could struggle to find work on the open market. As for McKenzie, we'll soon find out if misfires like Woodley will change how he approaches free agency.

The latest Around The NFL Podcast breaks down the annual "Top 101 free agents" list and discusses the latest in league news. Find more Around The NFL content on NFL NOW."

RG @thevelvetburritos: The next time you're thinking about getting a dog and consider a breeder or pet store as an ethically viable option, remember this face. This is the face of a shelter dog. This is the face of a pit bull mutt. This is the face of complete and utter velveteen seal-face sad-pants sausage-shark perfection. Shelter dogs come in all forms, ages and sizes, including both puppies and pure bred dogs. When 3000 dogs are killed each day because they don't have a home, there are no ethical reasons to purchase a dog (barring a therapy/working dog). Worried about temperamet? Get a dog that's been in a foster home for a few months so their true personality is known. Worried about health? Get a mutt, as their chances of developing heritable diseases are drasticly lower than a pure bred dog (pure bred inherently means less genetic diversity). Want a rare breed? Find a breed-specific rescue in your area or one that relocates. ğŸŒ€Ranks!ğŸŒ€
~
â¬Read below!â¬
~
King: Leads the pride with the queen. Can kick out any lion or lioness that is being rude or disobeying the Queen, King, Prince, or Princess.
Queen: Leads the pride with the King. Can do exactly what the King does.
Prince: Either the King and Queen's son or the Princess' mate. Can't do as much as the King or Queen but can still lead the pride at some points.
Princess: Is either the King and Queen's daughter or the Prince's mate. Can do what the Prince can do.
Lead Hunter: Leads the Hunters.
Lead Warrior: Leads the Fighters in battle.
Hunters: Hunt for the pride.
Warriors: Fight and train for the pride.
Trainees: Trains either to be a hunter or a warrior.
Cub sitters: Mostly pregnant lioness' or lioness' that are nursing. They watch Cubs if the mother is busy or if the mother is dead.
Cubs: Baby lions, become trainees when they are 6 moons.
Elders: Wise and sometimes weak lions and lioness' that have retired or that have been injured sevearly that they can not go on to be a fighter or Hunter anymore.

Subject: SELF WORTH (Very Deep!!!) In a brief conversation, a man asked a woman he was pursuing the question: 'What kind of man are you looking for?' She sat quietly for a moment before looking him in the eye & asking, 'Do you really want to know?' Reluctantly, he said, 'Yes. She began to expound, 'As a woman in this day & age, I am in a position to ask a man what can you do for me that I can't do for myself? I pay my own bills. I take care of my household without the help of any man... or woman for that matter. I am in the position to ask, 'What can you bring to the table?' The man looked at her. Clearly he thought that she was referring to money. She quickly corrected his thought & stated, 'I am not referring to money. I need something more. I need a man who is striving for excellence in every aspect of life. He sat back in his chair, folded his arms, & asked her to explain. She said, 'I need someone who is striving for excellence mentally because I need conversation & mental stimulation. I don't need a simple-minded man. I need someone who is striving for excellence spiritually because I don't need to be unequally yoked...believers mixed with unbelievers is a recipe for disaster. I need a man who is striving for excellence financially because I don't need a financial burden. I need someone who is sensitive enough to understand what I go through as a woman, but strong enough to keep me grounded. I need someone who has integrity in dealing with relationships. Lies and game-playing are not my idea of a strong man. I need a man who is family-oriented. One who can be the leader, priest and provider to the lives entrusted to him by God. I need someone whom I can respect. In order to be submissive, I must respect him. I cannot be submissive to a man who isn't taking care of his business. I have no problem being submissive...he just has to be worthy. And by the way, I am not looking for him...He will find me. He will recognize himself in me. Hey may not be able to"
